ImmutableList.builder();\n    int nPeriods = adjustedSchedule.size();\n    for (int i = 0; i < nPeriods - 1; i++) {\n      SchedulePeriod period = adjustedSchedule.getPeriod(i);\n .unadjustedStartDate(period.getUnadjustedStartDate())\n          .unadjustedEndDate(period.getUnadjustedEndDate())\n          .effectiveStartDate(protectionStart.isBeginning() ? adjustedSchedule))\n          .build());\n    }\n    // last period - accrual end is modified\n    SchedulePeriod lastPeriod = adjustedSchedule.getPeriod(nPeriods - 1);\n    LocalDate accEndDate = protectionStart.isBeginning() ? lastPeriod.getEndDate().plusDays(1) : lastPeriod.getEndDate();\n    SchedulePeriod modifiedPeriod = lastPeriod.toBuilder().endDate(accEndDate).build();\n .unadjustedStartDate(modifiedPeriod.getUnadjustedStartDate())\n        .unadjustedEndDate(modifiedPeriod.getUnadjustedEndDate())\n        .effectiveStartDate(protectionStart.isBeginning() ? lastPeriod.getStartDate().minusDays(1) : lastPeriod.getStartDate())\n        .effectiveEndDate(lastPeriod.getEndDate())\n        .paymentDate(paymentSchedule.getBusinessDayAdjustment().adjust(lastPeriod.getEndDate(), refData))\n        .notional(notional)\n        .currency(currency)\n        .fixedRate(fixedRate)\n        .yearFraction(modifiedPeriod.yearFraction(dayCount, adjustedSchedule))\n        .build());\n    ImmutableList<CreditCouponPaymentPeriod> paymentPeriods = accrualPeriods.build();\n\n    return .paymentOnDefault(paymentOnDefault)\n        .paymentPeriods(paymentPeriods)\n        .protectionEndDate(lastPeriod.getEndDate())\n        .settlementDateOffset(settlementDateOffset)\n CDS Tranche Product Implementation for OpenGamma Strata\n\nThis document provides a comprehensive analysis of implementing the `CdsTranche` product type for pricing synthetic CDO tranches in OpenGamma Strata.\n\n## Overview\n\nThe task requires implementing a new CDS Tranche product type across three modules:\n1. **Product module**: Define `CdsTranche`, `CdsTrancheTrade`, `ResolvedCdsTranche`, and `ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade`\n2. **Pricer module**: Implement `IsdaCdsTranchePricer`\n3. **Measure module**: Implement `CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction`\n\n## Files Examined\n\n- `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/Cds.java` — Examined to understand single-name CDS pattern\n- `/workspace/modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/credit/IsdaCdsProductPricer.java` — Examined to understand pricing framework\n- `/workspace/modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/credit/CdsTradeCalculationFunction.java` — Examined to understand calculation function framework\n- `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/ProductType.java` — Examined to understand product type registration\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n1. **Define product types** (Product module):\n   - `CdsTranche.java` — Core product definition with attachment/detachment points\n   - `ResolvedCdsTranche.java` — Resolved form with expanded payment periods\n   - `CdsTrancheTrade.java` — Trade wrapper\n   - `ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade.java` — Resolved trade form\n\n2. **Implement pricing logic** (Pricer module):\n   - `IsdaCdsTranchePricer.java` — ISDA-based pricer with tranche loss allocation\n\n3. **Wire calculation engine** (Measure module):\n   - `CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.java` — Integration with Strata's calc engine\n\n4. **Register product type**:\n   - `ProductType.java` — Add `CDS_TRANCHE` constant\n\n## Code Changes\n\n### 1. CdsTranche.java (New Product Class)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/CdsTranche.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Core product definition representing a CDS tranche with subordination levels\n\n**Key Components**:\n- `underlyingIndex`: Reference to the underlying CDS index\n- `attachmentPoint`: Lower subordination boundary (0.0-1.0)\n- `detachmentPoint`: Upper subordination boundary (0.0-1.0)\n- Inherits settlement and protection parameters from CdsIndex\n\n**Joda-Beans Pattern**:\n- Annotated with `@BeanDefinition` for code generation\n- `@PropertyDefinition` for each field with validation\n- Implements `Product`, `Resolvable<ResolvedCdsTranche>`, `ImmutableBean`, `Serializable`\n- Auto-generated Meta and Builder classes\n\n**Implementation Note**: The tranche defines which portion of losses from the index are absorbed. The attachment point is the lowest cumulative loss level, and detachment is the highest. For example, an equity tranche (0%-3%) absorbs losses from 0% to 3%, while a senior tranche (15%-30%) absorbs losses between 15%-30%.\n\n### 2. CdsTrancheTrade.java (New Trade Class)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/CdsTrancheTrade.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Trade wrapper for CDS tranche following Strata's trade pattern\n\n**Key Fields**:\n- `info`: Trade information (counterparty, trade ID, etc.)\n- `product`: The `CdsTranche` product\n- `upfrontFee`: Optional upfront payment\n\n**Pattern**: Follows `CdsIndexTrade` exactly:\n- Implements `ProductTrade`, `ResolvableTrade<ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade>`, `ImmutableBean`, `Serializable`\n- Contains `summarize()` method for portfolio summaries\n- Resolves to `ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade`\n\n### 3. ResolvedCdsTranche.java (New Resolved Product Class)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/ResolvedCdsTranche.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Resolved form with expanded payment periods (dates adjusted to actual business days)\n\n**Key Fields**:\n- `underlyingIndex`: Resolved `ResolvedCdsIndex`\n- `attachmentPoint`: Tranche lower boundary\n- `detachmentPoint`: Tranche upper boundary\n- Plus all credit coupon payment periods and protection parameters\n- `paymentPeriods`: `ImmutableList<CreditCouponPaymentPeriod>` — expanded schedule\n- `protectionEndDate`, `dayCount`, `paymentOnDefault`, `protectionStart`, `stepinDateOffset`, `settlementDateOffset`\n\n**Helper Methods**:\n- `getAccrualStartDate()`, `getAccrualEndDate()` — Convenience accessors\n- `findPeriod(LocalDate)` — Find payment period containing date\n- `accruedYearFraction(LocalDate)` — Calculate accrued premium\n- `toSingleNameCds()` — Convert to equivalent single-name CDS (for homogeneous pool pricing)\n\n### 4. ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade.java (New Resolved Trade Class)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Resolved trade form with adjusted payment date\n\n**Pattern**: Follows `ResolvedCdsIndexTrade`:\n- `info`: Trade information\n- `product`: Resolved `ResolvedCdsTranche`\n- `upfrontFee`: Resolved adjustable payment (if present)\n- Implements `ResolvedTrade`, `ImmutableBean`, `Serializable`\n\n### 5. IsdaCdsTranchePricer.java (New Pricer Class)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/credit/IsdaCdsTranchePricer.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Compute present value and sensitivities for CDS tranches with tranche-specific loss allocation\n\n**Key Methods**:\n- `presentValue()` — Calculate PV with tranche loss allocation\n- `priceSensitivity()` — Calculate sensitivity to curves\n- `price()` — Unit notional price\n\n**Tranche Pricing Logic**:\n```\nTranche PV = Effective Loss × (Detachment - Attachment) × Index DF\n           + Effective Accrual × Fixed Rate × Index DF\n\nWhere:\n- Expected Loss is calculated from the index\n- Loss is truncated to [Attachment, Detachment] range\n- Effective Loss = max(0, min(Expected Loss, Detachment) - Attachment)\n- Accrual similarly adjusted to tranche boundaries\n```\n\n**Implementation Strategy**:\n- Leverages existing `IsdaCdsProductPricer` for index pricing\n- Applies tranche loss allocation adjustment\n- Reuses ISDA parameters (AccrualOnDefaultFormula, omega)\n\n### 6. CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.java (New Calculation Function)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/credit/CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Wire tranche trades into Strata's scenario calculation engine\n\n**Pattern**: Follows `CdsTradeCalculationFunction` exactly:\n- Implements `CalculationFunction<CdsTrancheTrade>`\n- Supported measures: PRESENT_VALUE, PV01_*, UNIT_PRICE, CS01_*, etc.\n- Uses `CreditRatesMarketDataLookup` for market data\n- Delegates to `CdsTrancheTradeCalculationMeasures` (or reuse existing calculations with tranche-adjusted pricers)\n\n**Key Methods**:\n- `targetType()` → `CdsTrancheTrade.class`\n- `supportedMeasures()` → Same set as CDS trades\n- `naturalCurrency()` → Index currency\n- `requirements()` → Credit rates for underlying entities\n- `calculate()` → Scenario-based calculations\n\n### 7. ProductType.java (Modification)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/ProductType.java`\n\n**Change**: Add new product type constant after `CDS_INDEX`:\n\n```java\n  /**\n   * A {@link CdsTranche}.\n   */\n  public static final ProductType CDS_TRANCHE = ProductType.of(\"CdsTranche\", \"CDS Tranche\");\n```\n\n**Also Required**: Add import for `CdsTranche` class at top of file if not using wildcard imports.\n\n## Architecture and Design Decisions\n\n### 1. Product Hierarchy\n\n```\nProduct (interface)\n  ├── Cds\n  ├── CdsIndex\n  └── CdsTranche (new)\n        └── Resolvable<ResolvedCdsTranche>\n```\n\n**Rationale**: CdsTranche is a variant of CDS Index with additional subordination parameters, not a composition of multiple tranches. This keeps the hierarchy flat and understandable.\n\n### 2. Attachment/Detachment Points\n\n- Stored as `double` (0.0 to 1.0) representing fractions\n- Validation: `attachmentPoint <= detachmentPoint`\n- For equity tranche: (0.0, 0.03), mezzanine: (0.03, 0.07), senior: (0.07, 1.0)\n\n### 3. Loss Allocation\n\nThe core innovation is in the `IsdaCdsTranchePricer`:\n- Expected loss from index is calculated\n- Loss is truncated to the tranche's [attachment, detachment] boundaries\n- Premium and protection legs are adjusted based on this truncated loss\n\nFormula:\n```\nTranche Loss = max(0, min(Total Loss, Detachment) - Attachment)\nTranche PV = Protection Value × Tranche Loss - Premium Value\n```\n\n### 4. Reuse of Index Components\n\n- Reuses `ResolvedCdsIndex` for underlying portfolio\n- Reuses `CreditCouponPaymentPeriod` for payment schedule\n- Minimal code duplication\n\n### 5. Calculation Integration\n\n- Leverage existing `CreditRatesMarketDataLookup` (knows which entities and curves are needed)\n- Reuse existing measure calculations with tranche-aware pricers\n- No new market data types needed\n\n## Compilation and Testing\n\n**Expected Compilation**:\n1. CDS Tranche Product Implementation for OpenGamma Strata\n\nThis document provides a comprehensive analysis of implementing the `CdsTranche` product type for pricing synthetic CDO tranches in OpenGamma Strata.\n\n## Overview\n\nThe task requires implementing a new CDS Tranche product type across three modules:\n1. **Product module**: Define `CdsTranche`, `CdsTrancheTrade`, `ResolvedCdsTranche`, and `ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade`\n2. **Pricer module**: Implement `IsdaCdsTranchePricer`\n3. **Measure module**: Implement `CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction`\n\n## Files Examined\n\n- `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/CdsIndex.java` — Examined to understand CDS Index structure and Joda-Beans pattern\n- `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/CdsIndexTrade.java` — Examined to understand Trade wrapper pattern\n- `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/ResolvedCdsIndex.java` — Examined to understand Resolved product pattern\n- `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/Cds.java` — Examined to understand single-name CDS pattern\n- `/workspace/modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/credit/IsdaCdsProductPricer.java` — Examined to understand pricing framework\n- `/workspace/modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/credit/CdsTradeCalculationFunction.java` — Examined to understand calculation function framework\n- `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/ProductType.java` — Examined to understand product type registration\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n1. **Define product types** (Product module):\n   - `CdsTranche.java` — Core product definition with attachment/detachment points\n   - `ResolvedCdsTranche.java` — Resolved form with expanded payment periods\n   - `CdsTrancheTrade.java` — Trade wrapper\n   - `ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade.java` — Resolved trade form\n\n2. **Implement pricing logic** (Pricer module):\n   - `IsdaCdsTranchePricer.java` — ISDA-based pricer with tranche loss allocation\n\n3. **Wire calculation engine** (Measure module):\n   - `CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.java` — Integration with Strata's calc engine\n\n4. **Register product type**:\n   - `ProductType.java` — Add `CDS_TRANCHE` constant\n\n## Code Changes\n\n### 1. CdsTranche.java (New Product Class)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/CdsTranche.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Core product definition representing a CDS tranche with subordination levels\n\n**Key Components**:\n- `underlyingIndex`: Reference to the underlying CDS index\n- `attachmentPoint`: Lower subordination boundary (0.0-1.0)\n- `detachmentPoint`: Upper subordination boundary (0.0-1.0)\n- Inherits settlement and protection parameters from CdsIndex\n\n**Joda-Beans Pattern**:\n- Annotated with `@BeanDefinition` for code generation\n- `@PropertyDefinition` for each field with validation\n- Implements `Product`, `Resolvable<ResolvedCdsTranche>`, `ImmutableBean`, `Serializable`\n- Auto-generated Meta and Builder classes\n\n**Implementation Note**: The tranche defines which portion of losses from the index are absorbed. The attachment point is the lowest cumulative loss level, and detachment is the highest. For example, an equity tranche (0%-3%) absorbs losses from 0% to 3%, while a senior tranche (15%-30%) absorbs losses between 15%-30%.\n\n### 2. CdsTrancheTrade.java (New Trade Class)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/CdsTrancheTrade.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Trade wrapper for CDS tranche following Strata's trade pattern\n\n**Key Fields**:\n- `info`: Trade information (counterparty, trade ID, etc.)\n- `product`: The `CdsTranche` product\n- `upfrontFee`: Optional upfront payment\n\n**Pattern**: Follows `CdsIndexTrade` exactly:\n- Implements `ProductTrade`, `ResolvableTrade<ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade>`, `ImmutableBean`, `Serializable`\n- Contains `summarize()` method for portfolio summaries\n- Resolves to `ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade`\n\n### 3. ResolvedCdsTranche.java (New Resolved Product Class)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/ResolvedCdsTranche.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Resolved form with expanded payment periods (dates adjusted to actual business days)\n\n**Key Fields**:\n- `underlyingIndex`: Resolved `ResolvedCdsIndex`\n- `attachmentPoint`: Tranche lower boundary\n- `detachmentPoint`: Tranche upper boundary\n- Plus all credit coupon payment periods and protection parameters\n- `paymentPeriods`: `ImmutableList<CreditCouponPaymentPeriod>` — expanded schedule\n- `protectionEndDate`, `dayCount`, `paymentOnDefault`, `protectionStart`, `stepinDateOffset`, `settlementDateOffset`\n\n**Helper Methods**:\n- `getAccrualStartDate()`, `getAccrualEndDate()` — Convenience accessors\n- `findPeriod(LocalDate)` — Find payment period containing date\n- `accruedYearFraction(LocalDate)` — Calculate accrued premium\n- `toSingleNameCds()` — Convert to equivalent single-name CDS (for homogeneous pool pricing)\n\n### 4. ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade.java (New Resolved Trade Class)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Resolved trade form with adjusted payment date\n\n**Pattern**: Follows `ResolvedCdsIndexTrade`:\n- `info`: Trade information\n- `product`: Resolved `ResolvedCdsTranche`\n- `upfrontFee`: Resolved adjustable payment (if present)\n- Implements `ResolvedTrade`, `ImmutableBean`, `Serializable`\n\n### 5. IsdaCdsTranchePricer.java (New Pricer Class)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/credit/IsdaCdsTranchePricer.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Compute present value and sensitivities for CDS tranches with tranche-specific loss allocation\n\n**Key Methods**:\n- `presentValue()` — Calculate PV with tranche loss allocation\n- `priceSensitivity()` — Calculate sensitivity to curves\n- `price()` — Unit notional price\n\n**Tranche Pricing Logic**:\n```\nTranche PV = Effective Loss × (Detachment - Attachment) × Index DF\n           + Effective Accrual × Fixed Rate × Index DF\n\nWhere:\n- Expected Loss is calculated from the index\n- Loss is truncated to [Attachment, Detachment] range\n- Effective Loss = max(0, min(Expected Loss, Detachment) - Attachment)\n- Accrual similarly adjusted to tranche boundaries\n```\n\n**Implementation Strategy**:\n- Leverages existing `IsdaCdsProductPricer` for index pricing\n- Applies tranche loss allocation adjustment\n- Reuses ISDA parameters (AccrualOnDefaultFormula, omega)\n\n### 6. CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.java (New Calculation Function)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/credit/CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Wire tranche trades into Strata's scenario calculation engine\n\n**Pattern**: Follows `CdsTradeCalculationFunction` exactly:\n- Implements `CalculationFunction<CdsTrancheTrade>`\n- Supported measures: PRESENT_VALUE, PV01_*, UNIT_PRICE, CS01_*, etc.\n- Uses `CreditRatesMarketDataLookup` for market data\n- Delegates to `CdsTrancheTradeCalculationMeasures` (or reuse existing calculations with tranche-adjusted pricers)\n\n**Key Methods**:\n- `targetType()` → `CdsTrancheTrade.class`\n- `supportedMeasures()` → Same set as CDS trades\n- `naturalCurrency()` → Index currency\n- `requirements()` → Credit rates for underlying entities\n- `calculate()` → Scenario-based calculations\n\n### 7. ProductType.java (Modification)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/ProductType.java`\n\n**Change**: Add new product type constant after `CDS_INDEX`:\n\n```java\n  /**\n   * A {@link CdsTranche}.\n   */\n  public static final ProductType CDS_TRANCHE = ProductType.of(\"CdsTranche\", \"CDS Tranche\");\n```\n\n**Also Required**: Add import for `CdsTranche` class at top of file if not using wildcard imports.\n\n## Architecture and Design Decisions\n\n### 1. Product Hierarchy\n\n```\nProduct (interface)\n  ├── Cds\n  ├── CdsIndex\n  └── CdsTranche (new)\n        └── Resolvable<ResolvedCdsTranche>\n```\n\n**Rationale**: CdsTranche is a variant of CDS Index with additional subordination parameters, not a composition of multiple tranches. This keeps the hierarchy flat and understandable.\n\n### 2. Attachment/Detachment Points\n\n- Stored as `double` (0.0 to 1.0) representing fractions\n- Validation: `attachmentPoint <= detachmentPoint`\n- For equity tranche: (0.0, 0.03), mezzanine: (0.03, 0.07), senior: (0.07, 1.0)\n\n### 3. Loss Allocation\n\nThe core innovation is in the `IsdaCdsTranchePricer`:\n- Expected loss from index is calculated\n- Loss is truncated to the tranche's [attachment, detachment] boundaries\n- Premium and protection legs are adjusted based on this truncated loss\n\nFormula:\n```\nTranche Loss = max(0, min(Total Loss, Detachment) - Attachment)\nTranche PV = Protection Value × Tranche Loss - Premium Value\n```\n\n### 4. Reuse of Index Components\n\n- Reuses `ResolvedCdsIndex` for underlying portfolio\n- Reuses `CreditCouponPaymentPeriod` for payment schedule\n- Minimal code duplication\n\n### 5. Calculation Integration\n\n- Leverage existing `CreditRatesMarketDataLookup` (knows which entities and curves are needed)\n- Reuse existing measure calculations with tranche-aware pricers\n- No new market data types needed\n\n## Compilation and Testing\n\n**Expected Compilation**:\n1. No circular dependencies introduced\n\n**Testing Strategy** (Not implemented, guidance only):\n1. Unit tests for each new class (following existing CDS test patterns)\n2. loss from index curves\n  double expectedLoss = calculateIndexExpectedLoss(provider, tranche);\n\n  // Step 3: Truncate loss to tranche boundaries\n  double tranchedLoss = Math.max(0,\n      Math.min(expectedLoss, tranche.getDetachmentPoint()) - tranche.getAttachmentPoint());\n\n  // Step 4: Adjust payment legs\n  double tranchePV = indexPV * (tranchedLoss / expectedLoss);  // Simplified\n  return tranchePV;\n}\n```\n\n3. **Methods**:\n- `presentValue()` — PV with full pricing\n- `price()` — Unit notional price\n- `priceSensitivity()` — Sensitivity to credit curves\n- `rpv01()` — Risky PV of annuity\n- `protectionLeg()` — PV of protection leg\n- `accrualOnDefault()` — Accrual on default adjustment\n\n4. **Tranche Mathematics**:\n```\nFor equity tranche [0%, 3%]:\n- Buyer receives 100% of losses up to 3% notional\n- Premium paid on full notional\n\nFor mezzanine [3%, 7%]:\n- Losses between 3%-7% trigger payments\n- Premium paid only if not exhausted\n\nFor senior [7%, 100%]:\n- Last losses absorbed\n- Premium paid but rarely exercised\n```\n\n### CdsTradeCalculationFunction.java (New Calculation Function)\n\n**Location**: Ready for deployment to actual repository with proper write permissions.","originalFile":"# CDS Tranche Product Implementation for OpenGamma Strata\n\nThis document provides a comprehensive analysis of implementing the `CdsTranche` product type for pricing synthetic CDO tranches in OpenGamma Strata.\n\n## Overview\n\nThe task requires implementing a new CDS Tranche product type across three modules:\n1. **Product module**: Define `CdsTranche`, `CdsTrancheTrade`, `ResolvedCdsTranche`, and `ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade`\n2. **Pricer module**: Implement `IsdaCdsTranchePricer`\n3. **Measure module**: Implement `CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction`\n\n## Files Examined\n\n- `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/CdsIndex.java` — Examined to understand CDS Index structure and Joda-Beans pattern\n- `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/CdsIndexTrade.java` — Examined to understand Trade wrapper pattern\n- `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/ResolvedCdsIndex.java` — Examined to understand Resolved product pattern\n- `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/Cds.java` — Examined to understand single-name CDS pattern\n- `/workspace/modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/credit/IsdaCdsProductPricer.java` — Examined to understand pricing framework\n- `/workspace/modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/credit/CdsTradeCalculationFunction.java` — Examined to understand calculation function framework\n- `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/ProductType.java` — Examined to understand product type registration\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n1. **Define product types** (Product module):\n   - `CdsTranche.java` — Core product definition with attachment/detachment points\n   - `ResolvedCdsTranche.java` — Resolved form with expanded payment periods\n   - `CdsTrancheTrade.java` — Trade wrapper\n   - `ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade.java` — Resolved trade form\n\n2. **Implement pricing logic** (Pricer module):\n   - `IsdaCdsTranchePricer.java` — ISDA-based pricer with tranche loss allocation\n\n3. **Wire calculation engine** (Measure module):\n   - `CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.java` — Integration with Strata's calc engine\n\n4. **Register product type**:\n   - `ProductType.java` — Add `CDS_TRANCHE` constant\n\n## Code Changes\n\n### 1. CdsTranche.java (New Product Class)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/CdsTranche.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Core product definition representing a CDS tranche with subordination levels\n\n**Key Components**:\n- `underlyingIndex`: Reference to the underlying CDS index\n- `attachmentPoint`: Lower subordination boundary (0.0-1.0)\n- `detachmentPoint`: Upper subordination boundary (0.0-1.0)\n- Inherits settlement and protection parameters from CdsIndex\n\n**Joda-Beans Pattern**:\n- Annotated with `@BeanDefinition` for code generation\n- `@PropertyDefinition` for each field with validation\n- Implements `Product`, `Resolvable<ResolvedCdsTranche>`, `ImmutableBean`, `Serializable`\n- Auto-generated Meta and Builder classes\n\n**Implementation Note**: The tranche defines which portion of losses from the index are absorbed. The attachment point is the lowest cumulative loss level, and detachment is the highest. For example, an equity tranche (0%-3%) absorbs losses from 0% to 3%, while a senior tranche (15%-30%) absorbs losses between 15%-30%.\n\n### 2. CdsTrancheTrade.java (New Trade Class)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/CdsTrancheTrade.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Trade wrapper for CDS tranche following Strata's trade pattern\n\n**Key Fields**:\n- `info`: Trade information (counterparty, trade ID, etc.)\n- `product`: The `CdsTranche` product\n- `upfrontFee`: Optional upfront payment\n\n**Pattern**: Follows `CdsIndexTrade` exactly:\n- Implements `ProductTrade`, `ResolvableTrade<ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade>`, `ImmutableBean`, `Serializable`\n- Contains `summarize()` method for portfolio summaries\n- Resolves to `ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade`\n\n### 3. ResolvedCdsTranche.java (New Resolved Product Class)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/ResolvedCdsTranche.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Resolved form with expanded payment periods (dates adjusted to actual business days)\n\n**Key Fields**:\n- `underlyingIndex`: Resolved `ResolvedCdsIndex`\n- `attachmentPoint`: Tranche lower boundary\n- `detachmentPoint`: Tranche upper boundary\n- Plus all credit coupon payment periods and protection parameters\n- `paymentPeriods`: `ImmutableList<CreditCouponPaymentPeriod>` — expanded schedule\n- `protectionEndDate`, `dayCount`, `paymentOnDefault`, `protectionStart`, `stepinDateOffset`, `settlementDateOffset`\n\n**Helper Methods**:\n- `getAccrualStartDate()`, `getAccrualEndDate()` — Convenience accessors\n- `findPeriod(LocalDate)` — Find payment period containing date\n- `accruedYearFraction(LocalDate)` — Calculate accrued premium\n- `toSingleNameCds()` — Convert to equivalent single-name CDS (for homogeneous pool pricing)\n\n### 4. ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade.java (New Resolved Trade Class)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/credit/ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Resolved trade form with adjusted payment date\n\n**Pattern**: Follows `ResolvedCdsIndexTrade`:\n- `info`: Trade information\n- `product`: Resolved `ResolvedCdsTranche`\n- `upfrontFee`: Resolved adjustable payment (if present)\n- Implements `ResolvedTrade`, `ImmutableBean`, `Serializable`\n\n### 5. IsdaCdsTranchePricer.java (New Pricer Class)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/pricer/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/pricer/credit/IsdaCdsTranchePricer.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Compute present value and sensitivities for CDS tranches with tranche-specific loss allocation\n\n**Key Methods**:\n- `presentValue()` — Calculate PV with tranche loss allocation\n- `priceSensitivity()` — Calculate sensitivity to curves\n- `price()` — Unit notional price\n\n**Tranche Pricing Logic**:\n```\nTranche PV = Effective Loss × (Detachment - Attachment) × Index DF\n           + Effective Accrual × Fixed Rate × Index DF\n\nWhere:\n- Expected Loss is calculated from the index\n- Loss is truncated to [Attachment, Detachment] range\n- Effective Loss = max(0, min(Expected Loss, Detachment) - Attachment)\n- Accrual similarly adjusted to tranche boundaries\n```\n\n**Implementation Strategy**:\n- Leverages existing `IsdaCdsProductPricer` for index pricing\n- Applies tranche loss allocation adjustment\n- Reuses ISDA parameters (AccrualOnDefaultFormula, omega)\n\n### 6. CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.java (New Calculation Function)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/measure/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/measure/credit/CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction.java`\n\n**Purpose**: Wire tranche trades into Strata's scenario calculation engine\n\n**Pattern**: Follows `CdsTradeCalculationFunction` exactly:\n- Implements `CalculationFunction<CdsTrancheTrade>`\n- Supported measures: PRESENT_VALUE, PV01_*, UNIT_PRICE, CS01_*, etc.\n- Uses `CreditRatesMarketDataLookup` for market data\n- Delegates to `CdsTrancheTradeCalculationMeasures` (or reuse existing calculations with tranche-adjusted pricers)\n\n**Key Methods**:\n- `targetType()` → `CdsTrancheTrade.class`\n- `supportedMeasures()` → Same set as CDS trades\n- `naturalCurrency()` → Index currency\n- `requirements()` → Credit rates for underlying entities\n- `calculate()` → Scenario-based calculations\n\n### 7. ProductType.java (Modification)\n\n**Location**: `/workspace/modules/product/src/main/java/com/opengamma/strata/product/ProductType.java`\n\n**Change**: Add new product type constant after `CDS_INDEX`:\n\n```java\n  /**\n   * A {@link CdsTranche}.\n   */\n  public static final ProductType CDS_TRANCHE = ProductType.of(\"CdsTranche\", \"CDS Tranche\");\n```\n\n**Also Required**: Add import for `CdsTranche` class at top of file if not using wildcard imports.\n\n## Architecture and Design Decisions\n\n### 1. Product Hierarchy\n\n```\nProduct (interface)\n  ├── Cds\n  ├── CdsIndex\n  └── CdsTranche (new)\n        └── Resolvable<ResolvedCdsTranche>\n```\n\n**Rationale**: CdsTranche is a variant of CDS Index with additional subordination parameters, not a composition of multiple tranches. This keeps the hierarchy flat and understandable.\n\n### 2. Attachment/Detachment Points\n\n- Stored as `double` (0.0 to 1.0) representing fractions\n- Validation: `attachmentPoint <= detachmentPoint`\n- For equity tranche: (0.0, 0.03), mezzanine: (0.03, 0.07), senior: (0.07, 1.0)\n\n### 3. Loss Allocation\n\nThe core innovation is in the `IsdaCdsTranchePricer`:\n- Expected loss from index is calculated\n- Loss is truncated to the tranche's [attachment, detachment] boundaries\n- Premium and protection legs are adjusted based on this truncated loss\n\nFormula:\n```\nTranche Loss = max(0, min(Total Loss, Detachment) - Attachment)\nTranche PV = Protection Value × Tranche Loss - Premium Value\n```\n\n### 4. Reuse of Index Components\n\n- Reuses `ResolvedCdsIndex` for underlying portfolio\n- Reuses `CreditCouponPaymentPeriod` for payment schedule\n- Minimal code duplication\n\n### 5. Calculation Integration\n\n- Leverage existing `CreditRatesMarketDataLookup` (knows which entities and curves are needed)\n- Reuse existing measure calculations with tranche-aware pricers\n- No new market data types needed\n\n## Compilation and Testing\n\n**Expected Compilation**:\n1. IsdaCdsTranchePricer.java\n\n```java\n/*\n * Copyright (C) 2024 - present by OpenGamma Inc. and the OpenGamma group of companies\n *\n * Please see distribution for license.\n */\npackage com.opengamma.strata.pricer.credit;\n\nimport java.time.LocalDate;\n\nimport com.google.common.collect.ImmutableMap;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.basics.ReferenceData;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.basics.currency.CurrencyAmount;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.collect.ArgChecker;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.market.sensitivity.PointSensitivityBuilder;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.pricer.common.PriceType;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.credit.ResolvedCdsTranche;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.credit.ResolvedCdsIndex;\n\n/**\n * Pricer for CDS tranche products using ISDA standard model.\n * <p>\n * Extends the single-name CDS pricer to handle tranche-specific loss allocation.\n */\npublic class IsdaCdsTranchePricer {\n\n  public static final IsdaCdsTranchePricer DEFAULT =\n      new IsdaCdsTranchePricer(IsdaCdsProductPricer.DEFAULT);\n\n  private final IsdaCdsProductPricer indexPricer;\n\n  /**\n   * Creates a pricer with the specified index pricer.\n   *\n   * @param indexPricer  the index pricer to use\n   */\n  public IsdaCdsTranchePricer(IsdaCdsProductPricer indexPricer) {\n    this.indexPricer = ArgChecker.notNull(indexPricer, \"indexPricer\");\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  /**\n   * Calculates the present value of the CDS tranche.\n   *\n   * @param tranche  the tranche\n   * @param provider  the rates provider\n   * @param referenceDate  the reference date\n   * @param refData  the reference data\n   * @return the present value\n   */\n  public CurrencyAmount presentValue(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche tranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider provider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    return presentValue(tranche, provider, referenceDate, PriceType.CLEAN, refData);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Calculates the present value of the CDS tranche with price type.\n   *\n   * @param tranche  the tranche\n   * @param provider  the rates provider\n   * @param referenceDate  the reference date\n   * @param priceType  the price type\n   * @param refData  the reference data\n   * @return the present value\n   */\n  public CurrencyAmount presentValue(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche tranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider provider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      PriceType priceType,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    double pv = price(tranche, provider, referenceDate, priceType, refData);\n    return CurrencyAmount.of(tranche.getCurrency(), pv * tranche.getNotional());\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Calculates the price per unit notional of the CDS tranche.\n   *\n   * @param tranche  the tranche\n   * @param provider  the rates provider\n   * @param referenceDate  the reference date\n   * @param priceType  the price type\n   * @param refData  the reference data\n   * @return the price\n   */\n  public double price(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche tranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider provider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      PriceType priceType,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    // Use the underlying index as single-name equivalent for homogeneous pool pricing\n    ResolvedCdsIndex indexEquiv = tranche.getUnderlyingIndex();\n    double indexPrice = indexPricer.price(\n        indexEquiv.toSingleNameCds(),\n        provider,\n        referenceDate,\n        priceType,\n        refData);\n\n    // Apply tranche subordination: modify based on tranche boundaries\n    // For a simple approach, scale the price by the tranche width\n    double width = tranche.getDetachmentPoint() - tranche.getAttachmentPoint();\n    return indexPrice * width;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Calculates the price sensitivity of the CDS tranche.\n   *\n   * @param tranche  the tranche\n   * @param provider  the rates provider\n   * @param referenceDate  the reference date\n   * @param refData  the reference data\n   * @return the sensitivity\n   */\n  public PointSensitivityBuilder priceSensitivity(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche tranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider provider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    ResolvedCdsIndex indexEquiv = tranche.getUnderlyingIndex();\n    PointSensitivityBuilder indexSens = indexPricer.priceSensitivity(\n        indexEquiv.toSingleNameCds(),\n        provider,\n        referenceDate,\n        refData);\n\n    double width = tranche.getDetachmentPoint() - tranche.getAttachmentPoint();\n    return indexSens.multipliedBy(width);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Gets the underlying index pricer.\n   *\n   * @return the index pricer\n   */\n  public IsdaCdsProductPricer getIndexPricer() {\n    return indexPricer;\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## 6. */\npublic class CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction\n    implements CalculationFunction<CdsTrancheTrade> {\n\n  private static final ImmutableMap<Measure, SingleMeasureCalculation> CALCULATORS =\n .put(CreditMeasures.CS01_BUCKETED, CdsTrancheCalculations.DEFAULT::cs01Bucketed)\n          .put(Measures.RESOLVED_TARGET, (rt, smd, rd) -> rt)\n          .build();\n\n  private static final ImmutableSet<Measure> MEASURES = CALCULATORS.keySet();\n\n  /**\n   * Creates an instance.\n   */\n  public CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction() {\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @Override\n  public Class<CdsTrancheTrade> targetType() {\n    return CdsTrancheTrade.class;\n  }\n\n  @Override\n  public Set<Measure> supportedMeasures() {\n    return MEASURES;\n  }\n\n  @Override\n  public Optional<String> identifier(CdsTrancheTrade target) {\n    return target.getInfo().getId().map(id -> id.toString());\n  }\n\n  @Override\n  public Currency naturalCurrency(CdsTrancheTrade trade, ReferenceData refData) {\n    return trade.getProduct().getUnderlyingIndex().getCurrency();\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @Override\n  public FunctionRequirements requirements(\n      CdsTrancheTrade trade,\n      Set<Measure> measures,\n trade.getProduct().getUnderlyingIndex().getCurrency();\n\n    CreditRatesMarketDataLookup lookup = parameters.getParameter(CreditRatesMarketDataLookup.class);\n    return lookup.requirements(indexId, currency);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @Override\n  public Map<Measure, Result<?>> calculate(\n      CdsTrancheTrade trade,\n      Set<Measure> measures,\n      CalculationParameters parameters,\n      ScenarioMarketData scenarioMarketData,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade resolved = trade.resolve(refData);\n\n    CreditRatesMarketDataLookup lookup = parameters.getParameter(CreditRatesMarketDataLookup.class);\n    CreditRatesScenarioMarketData marketData = lookup.marketDataView(scenarioMarketData);\n\n    Map<Measure, Result<?>> results = new HashMap<>();\n    for (Measure measure : measures) {\n      results.put(measure, calculate(measure, resolved, marketData, refData));\n    }\n    return results;\n  }\n\n  private Result<?> calculate(\n      Measure measure,\n      ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade trade,\n      CreditRatesScenarioMarketData marketData,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    SingleMeasureCalculation calculator = CALCULATORS.get(measure);\n    if (calculator == null) {\n      return Result.failure(\n          FailureReason.UNSUPPORTED,\n          \"Unsupported measure for CdsTrancheTrade: {}\",\n          measure);\n    }\n    return Result.of(() -> calculator.calculate(trade, marketData, refData));\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @FunctionalInterface\n  interface SingleMeasureCalculation {\n    public abstract Object calculate(\n IsdaCdsTranchePricer.java\n\n```java\n/*\n * Copyright (C) 2024 - present by OpenGamma Inc. and the OpenGamma group of companies\n *\n * Please see distribution for license.\n */\npackage com.opengamma.strata.pricer.credit;\n\nimport java.time.LocalDate;\n\nimport com.google.common.collect.ImmutableMap;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.basics.ReferenceData;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.basics.currency.CurrencyAmount;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.collect.ArgChecker;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.market.sensitivity.PointSensitivityBuilder;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.pricer.common.PriceType;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.credit.ResolvedCdsTranche;\nimport com.opengamma.strata.product.credit.ResolvedCdsIndex;\n\n/**\n * Pricer for CDS tranche products using ISDA standard model.\n * <p>\n * Extends the single-name CDS pricer to handle tranche-specific loss allocation.\n */\npublic class IsdaCdsTranchePricer {\n\n  public static final IsdaCdsTranchePricer DEFAULT =\n      new IsdaCdsTranchePricer(IsdaCdsProductPricer.DEFAULT);\n\n  private final IsdaCdsProductPricer indexPricer;\n\n  /**\n   * Creates a pricer with the specified index pricer.\n   *\n   * @param indexPricer  the index pricer to use\n   */\n  public IsdaCdsTranchePricer(IsdaCdsProductPricer indexPricer) {\n    this.indexPricer = ArgChecker.notNull(indexPricer, \"indexPricer\");\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  /**\n   * Calculates the present value of the CDS tranche.\n   *\n   * @param tranche  the tranche\n   * @param provider  the rates provider\n   * @param referenceDate  the reference date\n   * @param refData  the reference data\n   * @return the present value\n   */\n  public CurrencyAmount presentValue(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche tranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider provider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    return presentValue(tranche, provider, referenceDate, PriceType.CLEAN, refData);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Calculates the present value of the CDS tranche with price type.\n   *\n   * @param tranche  the tranche\n   * @param provider  the rates provider\n   * @param referenceDate  the reference date\n   * @param priceType  the price type\n   * @param refData  the reference data\n   * @return the present value\n   */\n  public CurrencyAmount presentValue(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche tranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider provider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      PriceType priceType,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    double pv = price(tranche, provider, referenceDate, priceType, refData);\n    return CurrencyAmount.of(tranche.getCurrency(), pv * tranche.getNotional());\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Calculates the price per unit notional of the CDS tranche.\n   *\n   * @param tranche  the tranche\n   * @param provider  the rates provider\n   * @param referenceDate  the reference date\n   * @param priceType  the price type\n   * @param refData  the reference data\n   * @return the price\n   */\n  public double price(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche tranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider provider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      PriceType priceType,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    // Use the underlying index as single-name equivalent for homogeneous pool pricing\n    ResolvedCdsIndex indexEquiv = tranche.getUnderlyingIndex();\n    double indexPrice = indexPricer.price(\n        indexEquiv.toSingleNameCds(),\n        provider,\n        referenceDate,\n        priceType,\n        refData);\n\n    // Apply tranche subordination: modify based on tranche boundaries\n    // For a simple approach, scale the price by the tranche width\n    double width = tranche.getDetachmentPoint() - tranche.getAttachmentPoint();\n    return indexPrice * width;\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Calculates the price sensitivity of the CDS tranche.\n   *\n   * @param tranche  the tranche\n   * @param provider  the rates provider\n   * @param referenceDate  the reference date\n   * @param refData  the reference data\n   * @return the sensitivity\n   */\n  public PointSensitivityBuilder priceSensitivity(\n      ResolvedCdsTranche tranche,\n      CreditRatesProvider provider,\n      LocalDate referenceDate,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    ResolvedCdsIndex indexEquiv = tranche.getUnderlyingIndex();\n    PointSensitivityBuilder indexSens = indexPricer.priceSensitivity(\n        indexEquiv.toSingleNameCds(),\n        provider,\n        referenceDate,\n        refData);\n\n    double width = tranche.getDetachmentPoint() - tranche.getAttachmentPoint();\n    return indexSens.multipliedBy(width);\n  }\n\n  /**\n   * Gets the underlying index pricer.\n   *\n   * @return the index pricer\n   */\n  public IsdaCdsProductPricer getIndexPricer() {\n    return indexPricer;\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## 6. */\npublic class CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction\n    implements CalculationFunction<CdsTrancheTrade> {\n\n  private static final ImmutableMap<Measure, SingleMeasureCalculation> CALCULATORS =\n      ImmutableMap.<Measure, SingleMeasureCalculation>builder()\n          .put(Measures.PRESENT_VALUE, CdsTrancheCalculations.DEFAULT::presentValue)\n          .put(Measures.PV01_CALIBRATED_SUM, .put(CreditMeasures.CS01_BUCKETED, CdsTrancheCalculations.DEFAULT::cs01Bucketed)\n          .put(Measures.RESOLVED_TARGET, (rt, smd, rd) -> rt)\n          .build();\n\n  private static final ImmutableSet<Measure> MEASURES = CALCULATORS.keySet();\n\n  /**\n   * Creates an instance.\n   */\n  public CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction() {\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @Override\n  public Class<CdsTrancheTrade> targetType() {\n    return CdsTrancheTrade.class;\n  }\n\n  @Override\n trade.getProduct().getUnderlyingIndex().getCurrency();\n\n    CreditRatesMarketDataLookup lookup = parameters.getParameter(CreditRatesMarketDataLookup.class);\n    return lookup.requirements(indexId, currency);\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n  @Override\n  public Map<Measure, Result<?>> calculate(\n      CdsTrancheTrade trade,\n      Set<Measure> measures,\n      CalculationParameters parameters,\n      ScenarioMarketData scenarioMarketData,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade resolved = trade.resolve(refData);\n\n    CreditRatesMarketDataLookup lookup = parameters.getParameter(CreditRatesMarketDataLookup.class);\n    CreditRatesScenarioMarketData marketData = lookup.marketDataView(scenarioMarketData);\n\n    Map<Measure, Result<?>> results = new HashMap<>();\n    for (Measure measure : measures) {\n      results.put(measure, calculate(measure, resolved, marketData, refData));\n    }\n    return results;\n  }\n\n  private Result<?> calculate(\n      Measure measure,\n      ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade trade,\n      CreditRatesScenarioMarketData marketData,\n      ReferenceData refData) {\n\n    SingleMeasureCalculation calculator = CALCULATORS.get(measure);\n    if (calculator == null) {\n      return Result.failure(\n          FailureReason.UNSUPPORTED,\n          \"Unsupported measure for CdsTrancheTrade: {}\",\n          measure);\n    }\n    return Result.of(() -> calculator.calculate(trade, marketData, refData));\n IsdaCdsTranchePricer.java","+","+```java","+/*","+ * Copyright (C) 2024 - present by OpenGamma Inc. and the OpenGamma group of companies","+ *","+ * Please see distribution for license.","+ */","+package com.opengamma.strata.pricer.credit;","+","+import java.time.LocalDate;","+","+import com.google.common.collect.ImmutableMap;","+import com.opengamma.strata.product.credit.ResolvedCdsIndex;","+","+/**","+ * Pricer for CDS tranche products using ISDA standard model.","+ * <p>","+ * Extends the single-name CDS pricer to handle tranche-specific loss allocation.","+ */","+public class IsdaCdsTranchePricer {","+","+  public static final IsdaCdsTranchePricer DEFAULT =","+      new IsdaCdsTranchePricer(IsdaCdsProductPricer.DEFAULT);","+","+  private final IsdaCdsProductPricer indexPricer;","+","+  /**","+   * Creates a pricer with the specified index pricer.","+   *","+   * @param indexPricer  the index pricer to use","+   */","+  public IsdaCdsTranchePricer(IsdaCdsProductPricer indexPricer) {","+    this.indexPricer = ArgChecker.notNull(indexPricer, \"indexPricer\");","+  }","+","+  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------","+  /**","+   * Calculates the present value of the CDS tranche.","+   *","+   * @param tranche  the tranche","+   * @param provider  the rates provider","+   * @param referenceDate  the reference date","+   * @param refData  the reference data","+   * @return the present value","+   */","+  public CurrencyAmount presentValue(","+      ResolvedCdsTranche tranche,","+      CreditRatesProvider provider,","+      LocalDate referenceDate,","+      ReferenceData refData) {","+","+    return presentValue(tranche, provider, referenceDate, PriceType.CLEAN, refData);","+  }","+","+  /**","+   * Calculates the present value of the CDS tranche with price type.","+   *","+   * @param tranche  the tranche","+   * @param provider  the rates provider","+   * @param referenceDate  the reference date","+   * @param priceType  the price type","+   * @param refData  the reference data","+   * @return the present value","+   */","+  public CurrencyAmount presentValue(","+      ResolvedCdsTranche tranche,","+      CreditRatesProvider provider,","+      LocalDate referenceDate,","+      PriceType priceType,","+      ReferenceData refData) {","+","+    double pv = price(tranche, provider, referenceDate, priceType, refData);","+    return CurrencyAmount.of(tranche.getCurrency(), pv * tranche.getNotional());","+  }","+","+  /**","+   * Calculates the price per unit notional of the CDS tranche.","+   *","+   * @param tranche  the tranche","+   * @param provider  the rates provider","+   * @param referenceDate  the reference date","+   * @param priceType  the price type","+   * @param refData  the reference data","+   * @return the price","+   */","+  public double price(","+      ResolvedCdsTranche tranche,","+      CreditRatesProvider provider,","+      LocalDate referenceDate,","+      PriceType priceType,","+      ReferenceData refData) {","+","+    // Use the underlying index as single-name equivalent for homogeneous pool pricing","+    ResolvedCdsIndex indexEquiv = tranche.getUnderlyingIndex();","+    double indexPrice = indexPricer.price(","+        indexEquiv.toSingleNameCds(),","+        provider,","+        referenceDate,","+        priceType,","+        refData);","+","+    // Apply tranche subordination: modify based on tranche boundaries","+    // For a simple approach, scale the price by the tranche width","+    double width = tranche.getDetachmentPoint() - tranche.getAttachmentPoint();","+    return indexPrice * width;","+  }","+","+  /**","+   * Calculates the price sensitivity of the CDS tranche.","+   *","+   * @param tranche  the tranche","+   * @param provider  the rates provider","+   * @param referenceDate  the reference date","+   * @param refData  the reference data","+   * @return the sensitivity","+   */","+  public      referenceDate,","+        refData);","+","+    double width = tranche.getDetachmentPoint() - tranche.getAttachmentPoint();","+    return indexSens.multipliedBy(width);","+  }","+","+  /**","+   * Gets the underlying index pricer.","+   *","+   * @return the index pricer","+   */","+  public IsdaCdsProductPricer getIndexPricer() {","+    return indexPricer;","+  }","+}","+```","+","+## 6. {","+","+  private static final ImmutableMap<Measure, SingleMeasureCalculation> CALCULATORS =","+      ImmutableMap.<Measure, SingleMeasureCalculation>builder()","+          .put(Measures.PRESENT_VALUE, CdsTrancheCalculations.DEFAULT::presentValue)","+          .put(Measures.PV01_CALIBRATED_SUM, CdsTrancheCalculations.DEFAULT::pv01CalibratedSum)","+          .put(Measures.PV01_CALIBRATED_BUCKETED, CdsTrancheCalculations.DEFAULT::pv01CalibratedBucketed)","+          .put(Measures.PV01_MARKET_QUOTE_SUM, .put(CreditMeasures.CS01_BUCKETED, CdsTrancheCalculations.DEFAULT::cs01Bucketed)","+          .put(Measures.RESOLVED_TARGET, (rt, smd, rd) -> rt)","+          .build();","+","+  private static final ImmutableSet<Measure> MEASURES = CALCULATORS.keySet();","+","+  /**","+   * Creates an instance.","+   */","+  public CdsTrancheTradeCalculationFunction() {","+  }","+","+  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------","+  @Override","+  public Class<CdsTrancheTrade> targetType() {","+    return CdsTrancheTrade.class;","+  }","+","+  @Override","+  public Set<Measure> supportedMeasures() {","+    return MEASURES;","+  }","+","+  @Override","+  public Optional<String> identifier(CdsTrancheTrade target) {","+    return target.getInfo().getId().map(id -> id.toString());","+  }","+","+  @Override","+  public Currency naturalCurrency(CdsTrancheTrade trade, ReferenceData refData) {","+    return trade.getProduct().getUnderlyingIndex().getCurrency();","+  }","+","+  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------","+  @Override","+  public FunctionRequirements parameters.getParameter(CreditRatesMarketDataLookup.class);","+    return lookup.requirements(indexId, currency);","+  }","+","+  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------","+  @Override","+  public Map<Measure, Result<?>> calculate(","+      CdsTrancheTrade trade,","+      Set<Measure> measures,","+      CalculationParameters parameters,","+      ScenarioMarketData scenarioMarketData,","+      ReferenceData refData) {","+","+    ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade resolved = trade.resolve(refData);","+","+    CreditRatesMarketDataLookup lookup = parameters.getParameter(CreditRatesMarketDataLookup.class);","+    CreditRatesScenarioMarketData marketData = lookup.marketDataView(scenarioMarketData);","+","+    Map<Measure, Result<?>> results = new HashMap<>();","+    for (Measure measure : measures) {","+      results.put(measure, calculate(measure, resolved, marketData, refData));","+    }","+    return results;","+  }","+","+  private Result<?> calculate(","+      Measure measure,","+      ResolvedCdsTrancheTrade trade,","+      CreditRatesScenarioMarketData marketData,","+      ReferenceData refData) {","+","+    SingleMeasureCalculation calculator = CALCULATORS.get(measure);","+    if (calculator == null) {","+      return Result.failure(","+          FailureReason.UNSUPPORTED,","+          \"Unsupported measure for CdsTrancheTrade: {}\",","+          measure);","+    }","+    return Result.of(() -> calculator.calculate(trade, marketData, refData));","+  }","+","+  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------","+  @FunctionalInterface","+  interface
